				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Novae aliquot et ante hac non ita usitatae cantiones suavissimae, LV 1577.2 (Lassus, Orlande de)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>24 pieces
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Publication
</th>
<td>1577 - <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://opac.rism.info/metaopac/search?q=rism00000990036689&amp;db=251&amp;View=rism&amp;Language=en">Munich: Adam Berg</a></span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Bicinia&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Bicinia</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_2_voices&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For 2 voices</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_unaccompanied_voices&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For unaccompanied voices</a></span>; <span class="expandline" title="8 more..."><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Scores_featuring_the_voice&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Scores featuring the voice</a></span>; <h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Novae aliquot et ante hac non ita usitatae cantiones suavissimae
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Novae aliquot et ante hac non ita usitatae ad duas voces cantiones suavissimae, omnibus musicis summè utiles: necnon tyronibus quàm eius artis peritioribus summopere inservientes
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Lassus,_Orlande_de" title="Category:Lassus, Orlande de">Lassus, Orlande de</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>LV 1577.2&#160;; RISM A/I: L 902&#160;; <a href="/wiki/List_of_compositions_by_Orlande_de_Lassus#Publications" title="List of compositions by Orlande de Lassus" class="mw-redirect">B/I: 1577c</a>
</td></tr>
<tr class="udelonly" data-display="table-row">
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>None <small>[<span class="icatassign">force assignment</span>]</small>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>24 pieces
<ol><li> <i><a href="/wiki/Beatus_vir_qui_in_sapientia_morabitur_(Lassus,_Orlande_de)" title="Beatus vir qui in sapientia morabitur (Lassus, Orlande de)">Beatus vir qui in sapientia morabitur</a></i>, LV 592 (D dorian)
</li><li> Beatus homo qui invenit sapientiam, LV 593 (F dorian)
</li><li> Oculus non vidit, LV 594 (D dorian)
</li><li> Justus cor suum tradet, LV 595 (D dorian)
</li><li> Expectatio justorum, LV 596 (A phrygian)
</li><li> Qui sequitur me non ambulat, LV 597 (A phrygian)
</li><li> Justi tulerunt spolia impiorum, LV 598 (F major)
</li><li> Sancti mei, LV 599 (F major)
</li><li> Qui vult venire post me, LV 600 (F major)
</li><li> Serve bone et fidelis, LV 601 (G mixolydian)
</li><li> Fulgebunt justi, LV 602 (G mixolydian)
</li><li> Sicut rosa inter spinas, LV 603 (G mixolydian)
</li><li> Bicinium in G dorian, LV 604
</li><li> Bicinium in G dorian, LV 605
</li><li> Bicinium in G dorian, LV 606
</li><li> Bicinium in G dorian, LV 607
</li><li> Bicinium in G dorian, LV 608
</li><li> Bicinium in G dorian, LV 609
</li><li> Bicinium in E phrygian, LV 610
</li><li> Bicinium in F lydian, LV 611
</li><li> Bicinium in G mixolydian, LV 612
</li><li> Bicinium in G mixolydian, LV 613
</li><li> Bicinium in G mixolydian, LV 614
</li><li> Bicinium in G mixolydian, LV 615
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
